                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="epithet">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font"><a href="/wiki/Epithet" title="Epithet">Epithet</a>:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">"Sengoku the Buddha"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">仏のセンゴク</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Hotoke no Sengoku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, Funimation subs [151]: "Saint Sengoku")</span>;<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><br />"The Resourceful General"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">智将</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Chishō</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span><sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></div>

<section class="pi-item pi-group pi-border-color pi-collapse pi-collapse-open">
	<h2 class="pi-item pi-header pi-secondary-font pi-item-spacing pi-secondary-background"><span class="df-header">Devil Fruit</span></h2>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi,_Model:_Daibutsu" title="Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu">Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu</a></div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Human-Human Fruit, Model: Buddha</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Human, Great Buddha</div>
</div>

<div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype">
	
		<h3 class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</h3>
	
	<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a></div>
</div>

</section>
</aside>
</p><table class="nomobile dfbox mw-collapsible" style="color: #F6F676;">
<tbody><tr><th class="cs" style="background: #090264">Devil Fruit</th></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfname"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Japanese Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi,_Model:_Daibutsu" title="Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu">Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu</a></div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfename"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">English Name:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Human-Human Fruit, Model: Buddha</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dfmeaning"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Meaning:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font">Human, Great Buddha</div></div></td></tr>
<tr><td><div class="pi-item pi-data pi-item-spacing pi-border-color" data-source="dftype"><span class="pi-data-label pi-secondary-font">Type:</span>
<div class="pi-data-value pi-font"><a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a></div></div></td></tr>
</tbody></table>
<p><b>Sengoku the Buddha</b><sup id="cite_ref-romanized_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-romanized-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> is a former <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-intro_2-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-intro-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> succeeding <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a> and preceding <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-fleet_admiral_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fleet_admiral-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He retired from his leadership position after the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c594_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> but remained in the Marines as an <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Inspector_General" title="Marine Ranks">Inspector General</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Inspector_General_4-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Inspector_General-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He was also one of the major figures along with Kong, <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a> during the times when <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, the "Pirate King", was still alive, and still continues to be in the present, even after his retirement from the Marines. He raised both <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Rosinante" title="Donquixote Rosinante">Donquixote Rosinante</a> and <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a> like his own sons.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Due to his actions and his position in the Marines, he is one of the three main antagonists of the <a href="/wiki/Marineford_Arc" title="Marineford Arc">Marineford Arc</a>, alongside Sakazuki and <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Sengoku is a tall, fair-skinned, and muscular man with a long, braided goatee and a mustache. He is usually seen alongside his pet goat. His cap covers his hair, which is set in a large afro. His afro was revealed after using his Devil Fruit powers and having his cap knocked off. Ironically, prior to the timeskip, despite already being an elderly man upon his debut (being 77 years old at the time, thereby making him a year older than Garp and Rayleigh, both men being from his generation), Sengoku displayed little to no physical signs of his actual age, with his hair still not having grayed after 20 years.   
</p><p>He typically wears black-rimmed glasses and a white and gold full Marine admiral uniform that is adorned with medals. The most distinctive features of this uniform are a life-size seagull on top of his cap, and his oversized Marine coat which he wears like a cape. His coat has the kanji for justice, in blue, emblazoned on the back, and has unique colored cuffs, with his being white.
</p><p>Twenty years before the present storyline, when Sengoku was already an Admiral, he did not cover his afro and sported only a mustache. During his orders to Saul to bombard Ohara, he wore less regal-looking attire than he does in the present storyline: a simple black tank top, blue jeans, and his glasses, which is unlike a typical Admiral's formal suit. The only Marine-related attire he wore at the time was apparently his Marine coat, draped over like a cape.<sup id="cite_ref-c0_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c0-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> However, when he was fighting Shiki in Marineford, he was wearing a black double-breasted suit with a blue tie under his coat. Fourteen years ago, still as an Admiral, he is seen wearing a white suit with a floral button dress shirt underneath and begins to grow his trademark braided goatee, albeit much shorter than it is now.<sup id="cite_ref-c764_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c764-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> His epaulettes during his time as an Admiral were similar to Garp's, which were red and black, but he doesn't have black on it, and he never used red epaulets ever since he became Fleet Admiral.
</p><p>In his youth, he also did not cover his afro and he lacked a beard.
</p><p>As a child, Sengoku had his trademark afro, and he was seen wearing a karate uniform with a black belt tied on his waist.
</p><p>During the two-year timeskip, Sengoku aged with his hair turning gray, and has also grown sideburns. His former uniform is now replaced with a more casual wear during his retirement. He is wearing a dark blue shirt with red and green zig-zag patterns, orange tie with white marine shorts, and a Marine coat.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Games">Video Games</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Sengoku appears to be an exceedingly proud, enlightened, and intelligent man who was loyal to the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> and, up until the cover-up of the <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> incident, never questioned orders from them. He also will not accept any reason for letting a criminal go, and also has a habit of getting very irritated with failure. His motto is "Reigning Justice"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">君臨する正義</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Kunrinsuru Seigi</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-c764_14-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c764-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> in that he prioritizes upholding justice over all things, although he certainly does not shy away from actions that fall under the code of <a href="/wiki/Justice#Absolute_Justice" title="Justice">Absolute Justice</a>. From his view, the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> are just pirates,<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> though he notes how valuable they can be when the time comes. However, as the years went by, he appeared to be losing his faith in the government, shown after the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> when he was furious at the order from the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a> to suppress the second escape incident in Level 6 of Impel Down to save face and keep the faith of the people, thus placing nations in danger. This eventually led Sengoku to resign from the Marines.
</p><p>Before the Summit War, he was concerned over the movements of the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, and had followed their actions ever since they departed from <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>, though at the time his current concern was about the upcoming war against <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>, to the point that he brushed off the incident of the attack on a <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Celestial Dragon</a> and left it to the <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admirals</a>. Upon hearing about Luffy's break-in of <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>, Sengoku was so frustrated that he almost took it out on Garp,<sup id="cite_ref-MonkeyGrudge_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MonkeyGrudge-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> and had come close to losing his patience with the antics of the Monkey family in general.
</p><p>Sengoku also believed that a person's birth (with the consideration of the parents' reputation) is enough to determine the potential impact they could bring to the world if left unchecked, such as Ace being Roger's son<sup id="cite_ref-Ace_father_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ace_father-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and Luffy being Dragon's son. This is shown at Ace's execution, where one of the main reasons for Ace's execution was not just because he was a pirate, but because he was the son of <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, and Sengoku believed that Ace must be eliminated by any means necessary, even if that meant an all-out war with Whitebeard.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>His epithet, Sengoku the Buddha, may seem contradictory at best since throughout the course of the series, while he has shown himself to be an extremely calm, composed, collected man, he has also shown himself to be quite capable of anger and violence. <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a> remarked on this irony when the Seven Warlords of the Sea convened at Mary Geoise to choose a successor for Crocodile.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> However, with the revelation of his Devil Fruit power, it would seem his epithet's origins come from his fruit's ability, exactly like the three current admirals (although his is not an alias).
</p><p>He also appears to have some common sense, as shown when he ordered the Summit War to be put to an end and ordered the other Marines to tend to the wounded, in doing so he avoided further casualties and a potential conflict with the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a>. His <a href="/wiki/Justice#Absolute_Justice" title="Justice">justice</a> is not as uncompromising as <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a>'s, and it seems to be more of a mix of both absolute and moral justice, as he did hold a large speech about morality. Another hint of moral justice is also shown when he got infuriated when the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> decided to cover up the mass escape of the Level 6 <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a> prisoners released by Blackbeard, although he once said not to question the World Government's orders.
</p><p>In addition, in his conversation with <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>, he stated that <a href="/wiki/Justice" title="Justice">justice</a> is a matter of personal values and does not endorse one form of justice over the other, mirroring <a href="/wiki/Smoker" title="Smoker">Smoker</a>'s talk with <a href="/wiki/Tashigi" title="Tashigi">Tashigi</a> in <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta</a>. This insinuates that Sengoku is more of a pragmatist in applying justice. <a href="/wiki/Caesar_Clown" title="Caesar Clown">Caesar Clown</a> also states Sengoku is too soft for rejecting the potential of mass-murder weapons and experimentation on prisoners, in contrast to what Caesar believes <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a> would want,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> further enforcing that Sengoku is more moral than he appears.
</p><p>After becoming an Inspector General, Sengoku seems to have become far more cheerful and laid-back and tends to take things very casually like his friend Garp, such as how he merely laughed playfully when Fujitora voiced his thoughts in how Law and Luffy should be acknowledged as Dressrosa's heroes, along with the Admiral's decision to not arrest the pirate alliance immediately. Tsuru notes this drastic change in Sengoku's behavior is the result of how he has less responsibilities as compared to his time in the past.<sup id="cite_ref-c796_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c796-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> Regardless, he still shows wisdom as he passed down his knowledge to the current generation of Marines about the past regarding the Four Emperors and pointed out how many world known figures have some affiliation with Wano.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Sengoku_Cries.png/revision/latest?cb=20160522202541" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Cries" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="212" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Cries.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Cries.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Sengoku_Cries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160522202541" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Sengoku_Cries.png/revision/latest?cb=20160522202541" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Cries" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Sengoku_Cries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160522202541" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="212" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Cries.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Cries.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/10/Sengoku_Cries.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20160522202541" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Cries.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku weeping inconsolably at the news of Rosinante's death.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Though he may appear to be stern because of his duties as a Marine, he is actually very kind and compassionate. His drastic actions at the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> were motivated by the desire to protect innocent civilians from getting embroiled in conflict out of fear that when the secrets held in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> are discovered, it would turn the world on its head and lead to total war. He also expressed extreme rage towards the World Government for trying to cover up the breakout of extremely dangerous criminals imprisoned in Level Six of Impel Down, as letting such criminals loose could pose immense danger to civilians. Furthermore, learning about <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Rosinante" title="Donquixote Rosinante">Donquixote Rosinante</a>'s death, a man he considered like his own son, was enough to break his heart and drive him to tears.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the death of <a href="/wiki/T_Bone" title="T Bone">T Bone</a>, Sengoku retained his serious demeanor when necessary, in spite of his laziness. He showed concerned for the civilians and how they attacked the Marines due to the influences of <a href="/wiki/Cross_Guild" title="Cross Guild">Cross Guild</a>. 
</p><p>Like his longtime colleague Garp, Sengoku's favorite snack is <i>okaki</i>, fried rice crackers. He is often seen munching on them, especially in his retirement. Like Issho, Sengoku's second favorite snack is a Soba Noodles.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marines">Marines</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Garp">Monkey D. Garp</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_and_Sengoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku's annoyance at Garp.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p><a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a> is a lifetime colleague of Sengoku's, having occasionally accompanied him on his assignments when he was still an Admiral, and even then, Sengoku found him irritating.<sup id="cite_ref-c0_13-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c0-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> As Garp is considered a "Hero of the Marines", Sengoku respects him greatly. However, their relationship was tested after discovering that Garp withheld the information that the infamous <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> is his grandson, which left the Fleet Admiral furious at Garp. This, added to the frustration caused by Luffy's repeated actions against the World Government, caused Sengoku to start losing patience with Garp and he made it clear he would have forced him to take responsibility if it were not for his position as the Hero of the Marines. Garp, on the other hand, took the development happily, much to Sengoku's frustration.<sup id="cite_ref-MonkeyGrudge_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MonkeyGrudge-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sengoku had somehow found out that Garp had adopted <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a>, the son of Pirate King <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, which was meant to be kept secret from the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a>. Sengoku warned Garp not to do anything foolish regarding Ace's execution, or there would be no mercy.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Sengoku also knows that the <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary</a> known as <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Dragon</a> is Luffy's father, and by extension Garp's son. It is unknown as to how long Sengoku knew about all this, or when he first learned about this, or how it would affect Garp's standing in the Marines. However, Sengoku had no problem in revealing everything to the entire world.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> When Garp allows Luffy to pass him, Sengoku was displeased, saying that Garp was in the end "still a grandfather". When Garp stood up after being hit by Luffy, he asked him whether he was alright, showing some concern. Sengoku is also quick to restrain Garp if he tries to do anything foolish, as shown when Sengoku pinned Garp to the ground when he later tried to go after Akainu for killing Ace.
</p><p>Despite being Garp's superior officer, Sengoku nonetheless carries a great deal of respect and still considers him to be an important friend and ally.
</p><p>After the Summit War, both Sengoku and Garp retired from their position but their records remained intact. Sengoku asked Hina of Garp's whereabouts since the new flavor Rice Crackers came out only to learned that he and SWORD have sailed to Hachinosu to rescue Koby.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tsuru">Tsuru</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku appears to be well-acquainted with Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> as well. Thirteen years ago, in the <a href="/wiki/North_Blue" title="North Blue">North Blue</a>, she worked under Sengoku's orders to stop the Donquixote Pirates. Despite being outranked by him, Tsuru still had no problem calling him a fool for providing her wrong intel.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Nowadays, Tsuru appears to be annoyed with Sengoku's new cheerful disposition and lack of responsibility that is almost similar to Garp.<sup id="cite_ref-c796_20-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c796-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kuzan">Kuzan</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku seems to show great respect for the former <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> and appreciates his view on justice as well as his potential for leadership. This was proven when he personally nominated <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a> to replace him in the position of Fleet Admiral, when he decided to step down himself.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Issho">Issho</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku seems to show respect for the newly promoted <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> and respects his view on justice. He does not berate <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Issho</a> for his choice to expose the abuse of the Warlord of the Sea position by <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a> to the general public. Despite this, the former <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a> does lightly suggest that Issho apologize to <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a> to mitigate the punishment he received for his refusal to suppress the Government's decision to permit the Heavenly Demon to usurp the Dressrosa throne.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku seems to be casual with his successor to the position of Fleet Admiral. He is amused when Issho uses a loophole to attend the Levely and comments to Akainu on how difficult it is to lead the Marines. When Sakazuki interrupted his meeting with the young Marines, Sengoku is not bothered at all and talked to his successor about <a href="/wiki/Kouzuki_Oden" title="Kouzuki Oden">Kouzuki Oden</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Donquixote_Rosinante">Donquixote Rosinante</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0d/Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20150823155227" class="image"><img alt="Rosinante Meets Sengoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Rosinante Meets Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0d/Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150823155227" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0d/Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20150823155227" class="image"><img alt="Rosinante Meets Sengoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0d/Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150823155227" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Rosinante Meets Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/0d/Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20150823155227" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Rosinante_Meets_Sengoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku's first meeting with Rosinante.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Despite being the last remaining relative of the pirate and future Warlord of the Sea <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, Sengoku had great trust in <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Rosinante" title="Donquixote Rosinante">Rosinante</a>, as Doflamingo was unknowingly being monitored by his younger brother. When Rosinante was 8 years old, Sengoku took him under his wing and later helped him become a Marine.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> It was implied that Sengoku was responsible for Corazon's façade of hating kids, in a ploy to discourage children from being drawn to and staying with the <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Pirates" title="Donquixote Pirates">Donquixote Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c764_14-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c764-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sengoku always saw Rosinante as a son and was devastated when his death was reported. Because of this, and with Rosinante lying to Sengoku just once regarding to the <a href="/wiki/Minion_Island" title="Minion Island">Minion Island</a> incident, Sengoku would later converse with <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Trafalgar Law</a> to confirm how and why Rosinante died and was able to get some closure upon learning the circumstances.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="X_Drake">X Drake</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After he fled his father's crew Sengoku took in Drake and treated him like his son.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="World_Government">World Government</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Twenty-two years ago, Sengoku was shown to be loyal to the World Government and did not like anyone questioning them. However, he has now lost his trust in them, especially the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a>, concerning the suppression of the Impel Down incident. This was proven by showing how angry he was at the government's decision not to issue bounties on the many criminals who had escaped from Level 6 of Impel Down. This is also shown by his outburst at their decision to keep quiet about the breakout, even though any one of the escapees could potentially destroy a country. This was one of, if not the biggest reason, for his retirement from the Marines.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Edward_Newgate">Edward Newgate</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As Sengoku was a major figure back in <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>'s time, and still is today, he is one of the few enemies <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> respects. Sengoku, along with the entire Marines and World Government, waged war against Whitebeard over the life of <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> before the latter's death. With the Marines' victory, Sengoku respected Shanks' wish to relinquish the bodies of Whitebeard and Ace for a proper burial, as opposed to showing them on the televised broadcast as trophies. By Shanks' admission, the Fleet Admiral respected the old pirate. In his meeting with <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>, Sengoku acknowledged Whitebeard to be the greatest of all legendary pirates.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marshall_D._Teach">Marshall D. Teach</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku shows a great deal of hatred towards <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a> for a number of reasons. These reasons include abandoning his post in Marineford, stealing a warship, infiltrating Impel Down, recruiting a number of extremely dangerous prisoners into his crew, abusing his position in the Seven Warlords of the Sea and later resigning from it, obtaining the power of the <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">Gura Gura no Mi</a>, and attempting to completely destroy Marineford.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Before resigning from the Marines, Sengoku was angry with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>'s actions such as defeating Warlord of the Sea <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a>, invading <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a> and defeating <a href="/wiki/Rob_Lucci" title="Rob Lucci">Rob Lucci</a> of the <a href="/wiki/CP9" title="CP9">CP9</a>, defeating Warlord of the Sea <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>, punching <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Noble</a> Saint <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a>, breaking into and out of <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>, and intruding on the war against Whitebeard in an attempt to rescue Ace. Coupled with the fact that each action deals a devastating blow to the World Government and that he is also <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a>'s grandson, Sengoku tended to take the frustration he felt after one of Luffy's stunts out on Garp. Sengoku also knows that Dragon is Luffy's biological father and considered the young pirate to be a great threat to the world due to his heritage, which is exactly the same way he felt about Ace. 
</p><p>After the timeskip, he seems to no longer show any animosity towards Luffy, as he did not reprimand Issho for letting Luffy and Law escape Dressrosa.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shanks">Shanks</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a> being a pirate, which would make him an enemy, Sengoku appears to have some respect towards him, stating that because of his words, he would officially end the war with the Whitebeard Pirates as well as hand over Ace and Whitebeard's bodies to the <a href="/wiki/Red_Hair_Pirates" title="Red Hair Pirates">Red Hair Pirates</a> to be given a proper burial. This is the first time Sengoku has shown respect towards a pirate, whereas he would not show respect even towards the Seven Warlords of the Sea.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shiki">Shiki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku seemed to view <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> as his main enemy twenty years ago in the same sense that Garp viewed Gol D. Roger. He warned Garp that Shiki was his to capture and was annoyed when Garp said he would give him the credit, showing Sengoku felt the need to capture Shiki himself and wasn't merely after fame. Although he was willing to fight Shiki with Garp when he attacked Marineford, this could be to limit the damage Shiki could cause seeing as he destroyed half of Marineford when fighting both of them.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Trafalgar_D._Water_Law">Trafalgar D. Water Law</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Despite being on opposite sides of the law, they both cared for the same person, Donquixote Rosinante, and currently honor his memory in their own different ways. Sengoku told <a href="/wiki/Trafalgar_D._Water_Law" title="Trafalgar D. Water Law">Law</a> that he should live because Rosinante sacrificed himself for the pirate. Perhaps because of Rosinante's actions, Sengoku decided to let Law leave Dressrosa, under the claim that he (Sengoku) is no longer a field officer, and therefore not obligated to arrest the renegade warlord.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sengoku was surprised to discover that Law was a <a href="/wiki/Will_of_D." title="Will of D.">D</a>, but apparently claimed that he knew nothing about the unique meaning of the letter.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jack">Jack</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As the Marines transferred <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a> toward <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a> attempted to rescue him at any costs. Sengoku's reputation was not enough for Jack to take back Doflamingo by force.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>As with <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Smoker" title="Smoker">Smoker</a> and <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a>, Sengoku believes that the <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Seven Warlords of the Sea</a> are no more than pirates, and therefore, trusts them very little, made clear when he called them "<i>scum of the sea</i>". However, he sees them as being very useful in times of need. When these World Government allies refuse to live up to their duties, such as <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a> did, Sengoku shows his resentment. Surprisingly, despite being informed about the exposure of <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>'s criminal enterprises on Dressrosa, he does not seem enraged and casually discusses the fiasco (although this was when Sengoku is semi-retired and was no longer as responsible).
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Others">Others</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kong">Kong</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku and <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a> are acquainted with each other even after Kong become the Commander-in-Chief for the World Government. Sengoku once worked under him when Kong was Fleet Admiral during Roger's time. After the Marineford War, Kong reassigned Sengoku as Inspector General after he succeeded in persuading Sengoku to stay in the Marines.
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><p><small>
<span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span></small></p><small><div style="float:right;">[<a href="#zephyr">skip section</a>]</div></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Z">Z</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D28&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku and <a href="/wiki/Z" title="Z">Z</a> were once friends until Z resigned from the Marines after the World Government allied with <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">pirates</a>. Sengoku stood silently for his former friend even after his attempting to destroy the new world.
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;" id="zephyr"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D29&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>As the former <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a> of the entire Marine force, Sengoku had absolute power over every action the Marines do, including summoning a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a>, granting and removing a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord</a>'s title at any time, provided they meet the criteria for either. The only ones that are above him are <a href="/wiki/Imu" title="Imu">Imu</a> (in secret), the <a href="/wiki/Five_Elders" title="Five Elders">Five Elders</a>, and Commander-in-Chief <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>. However, with his resignation, came the loss of such authorities.
</p><p>Alongside <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a>, Sengoku is one of the most powerful Marines of his generation. Both <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a> and <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a> held high regard for him. After defeating a group of Marines, Roger commented that he was one of the two Marines that were worth his time, the other being Garp.
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> was wreaking havoc in Marineford twenty-four years ago, Sengoku fought alongside Garp and were able to subdue him whilst destroying half the city in the process, keeping him imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>, a tremendous feat as Shiki is an immensely powerful swordsman who had single-handedly slaughtered an entire army of Marines before they subjugated him.<sup id="cite_ref-c0_13-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c0-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Even at 79 years old, Sengoku could, alongside <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Fujitora</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a>,&#160;defeat <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, one of the top-ranking, strongest members of the <a href="/wiki/Beasts_Pirates" title="Beasts Pirates">Beasts Pirates</a> under the Emperor <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c806_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c806-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D30&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>An extraordinary master strategist with immense military experience, Sengoku is renowned for his tactical and strategic genius by Marines and pirates alike. He is mainly responsible for all the Marine maneuvers deployed throughout the Whitebeard War at Marineford, such as forwarding a plan to all Marines that <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> was to be executed ahead of the official schedule with the intention that the opposing pirate forces would intercept the message and lose their composure. He then conspired with Admiral <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Akainu</a> in a plot to derail the alliance between Whitebeard's core divisions and the 41 independent New World pirate crews assisting by directing a 20-strong Pacifista division to target only the non-Whitebeard division pirates, and it was possible that the earlier transmissions regarding Ace's true parentage was not only an act of public justification but also to demoralize those pirates who were undermined by the Roger Pirates. With Akainu's persuasion, Sengoku's plan managed to drive one of those captains to attempt assassinating Whitebeard himself, and while the blow was not fatal, it did further debilitate Whitebeard's already hazardous condition.
</p><p>He operated his strategies while keeping close in mind the various powers of his greatest subordinates, especially the Marine Admirals: raising Marineford's siege walls in conjunction with Akainu's "Ryusei Kazan" to rout the allied pirate forces and destroying Whitebeard's flagship, the <a href="/wiki/Moby_Dick" title="Moby Dick">Moby Dick</a> while protecting the brunt of the Marine garrison from the damage.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D31&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Even without his Zoan Devil Fruit powers, Sengoku has enormous strength, enough to effortlessly hold down an enraged Garp with only one hand. Sengoku is also a tremendously skilled hand-to-hand fighter. Combined with his Mythical Zoan Devil Fruit powers, he could knock away all the members of the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>, who are extremely powerful in their own right, sending them flying.
</p><p>Sengoku has extraordinary speed, even in his gigantic buddha form. He could launch an unexpected surprise attack on all the members of the Blackbeard Pirates.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Devil_Fruit">Devil Fruit</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D32&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi,_Model:_Daibutsu" title="Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu">Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240813213645" class="image"><img alt="Hito Hito no Mi, Model Daibutsu Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="147" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hito Hito no Mi, Model Daibutsu Infobox.png" data-image-key="Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240813213645" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20240813213645" class="image"><img alt="Hito Hito no Mi, Model Daibutsu Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240813213645" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="147" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hito Hito no Mi, Model Daibutsu Infobox.png" data-image-key="Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/45/Hito_Hito_no_Mi%2C_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240813213645" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hito_Hito_no_Mi,_Model_Daibutsu_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku transforms with his Devil Fruit.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sengoku ate the Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu, a <a href="/wiki/Zoan#Mythical_Zoan" title="Zoan">Mythical Zoan</a>-type <a href="/wiki/Devil_Fruit" title="Devil Fruit">Devil Fruit</a> that allows him to transform into a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Daibutsu" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Daibutsu">giant golden Buddha</a> and a human-Buddha hybrid at will. This power is the source of his nickname, "Sengoku the Buddha". A number of Marines claimed that they have never seen him use this power before the war.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a Zoan, Sengoku gains an immense boost to his already impressive physical abilities while in his Buddha form. With only a single indirectly connecting punch, Sengoku was able to make the Marineford execution platform collapse, despite the punch being cushioned and blocked by Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques">Gear 3 inflated belly</a> and Mr. 3's "stronger than steel" <a href="/wiki/Doru_Doru_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Doru Doru no Mi">Candle Wall</a>.
</p><p>He can also release an exceptionally powerful golden shockwave with a palm thrust, it is strong enough to send a majority of the incredibly strong Blackbeard Pirates, consisting of some of the most dangerous criminals in history, flying a fair distance away. In the anime, his golden shockwaves are strong enough to clash evenly with the tremor shockwaves created by the <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">Gura Gura no Mi</a> of <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Haki">Haki</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D33&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<dl><dd><div class="noprint"><i>Main article&#58; <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a></i></div></dd></dl>
<p>As a former <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a> and leader of the Marines, Sengoku is fully capable of using Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-vicehaki_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vicehaki-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> He is also one of the very few people in the world who can use all three types of Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While he has not showcased <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King</a>, <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Haki/Observation_Haki" title="Haki/Observation Haki">Observation Haki</a> in the manga yet, he has utilized Armament Haki in the game <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Burning_Blood" title="One Piece: Burning Blood">One Piece: Burning Blood</a></i>.
</p>
