<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Video_Game_Only_Techniques">Video Game Only Techniques</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><b>Artillery Order</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"></span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>: Sengoku uses a <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Den Den Mushi</a> to call in an artillery strike on his opponent. Appears as one of Sengoku's Special Attacks in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Burning_Blood" title="One Piece: Burning Blood">One Piece: Burning Blood</a></i>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Not much is known about Sengoku's early life, other than he is originally from the <a href="/wiki/South_Blue" title="South Blue">South Blue</a> and joined the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> 56 years ago along with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Monkey D. Garp</a> and <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a>, at the age of 23.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> Over the years, Sengoku rose up through the ranks of the Marines, eventually achieving the rank of <a href="/wiki/Admiral" title="Admiral">Admiral</a> at some point before the Great Age of Pirates. 
</p><p>Thirty-one years ago, Sengoku met an 8-year-old <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Rosinante" title="Donquixote Rosinante">Donquixote Rosinante</a>, who was grieving the death of his father at the hands of his older brother <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Doflamingo</a>. Sengoku took the boy under his wing, coming to see him as a son. Rosinante eventually joined the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Encounter_with_Shiki_the_Golden_Lion">Encounter with Shiki the Golden Lion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D38&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png/revision/latest?cb=20240627013327" class="image"><img alt="Shiki and Sengoku and Garp" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Shiki and Sengoku and Garp.png" data-image-key="Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240627013327" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png/revision/latest?cb=20240627013327" class="image"><img alt="Shiki and Sengoku and Garp" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240627013327" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Shiki and Sengoku and Garp.png" data-image-key="Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2e/Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20240627013327" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Shiki_and_Sengoku_and_Garp.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> fight <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Twenty-seven years before the current storyline, the Marines were alerted to <a href="/wiki/Battle_in_Edd_War" class="mw-redirect" title="Battle in Edd War">a confrontation</a> between <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> and <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gol D. Roger</a>, and the then-Admiral Sengoku, Garp, and several other high-ranking Marines were sent on a mission to contain it. Before they could make it, a storm occurred, and half of Shiki's fleet was sunk during the battle. Three years later, Roger turned himself over to the Marines, and his execution was announced across the world. A week before Roger's execution, Shiki attacked <a href="/wiki/Marineford" title="Marineford">Marineford</a>, demanding that he be allowed to kill Roger. Sengoku and Garp intervened and fought him together. After a fierce battle that destroyed half of Marineford, they managed to defeat Shiki, and he was imprisoned in <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c0_13-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c0-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ohara_Incident">Ohara Incident</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D39&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Twenty-two years before the current storyline, Sengoku received orders from the <a href="/wiki/World_Government" title="World Government">World Government</a> to carry out a secret mission. This mission was to send a <a href="/wiki/Buster_Call" title="Buster Call">Buster Call</a> to obliterate <a href="/wiki/Ohara" title="Ohara">Ohara</a>. With these orders, Sengoku gave the <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi#Golden_Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Golden Den Den Mushi</a> for the operation to <a href="/wiki/CP9" title="CP9">CP9</a> director who was to investigate the situation, <a href="/wiki/Spandine" title="Spandine">Spandine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Admiral_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Admiral-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Among the five <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral" title="Vice Admiral">Vice Admirals</a> Sengoku chose to lead the Buster Call were <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a>, <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Kuzan</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Jaguar_D._Saul" title="Jaguar D. Saul">Jaguar D. Saul</a>.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png/revision/latest?cb=20161104023820" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Orders Saul" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Orders Saul.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161104023820" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png/revision/latest?cb=20161104023820" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Orders Saul" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161104023820" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Orders Saul.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2c/Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20161104023820" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Orders_Saul.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Admiral Sengoku telling Saul of his mission to <a href="/wiki/Ohara" title="Ohara">Ohara</a>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Following the arrest of <a href="/wiki/Nico_Olvia" title="Nico Olvia">Nico Olvia</a>, Sengoku notified Saul of his role in the upcoming mission. The <a href="/wiki/Giants" title="Giants">giant</a> protested against this and tried to reason with Sengoku that the Oharans were merely scholars interested only in history. Sengoku, however, ignored his protests and told Saul to just follow orders. Later, Sengoku received news that Saul had liberated Olvia from her imprisonment. Seeing that the Buster Call mission to Ohara was in jeopardy, Sengoku ordered his subordinates to quickly find the two before the operation could be stopped.<sup id="cite_ref-c396_29-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c396-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After the operation had finished, Sengoku was informed by Spandine that one of the scholars of Ohara had escaped from the Buster Call attack. This little girl, <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>, was deemed a threat. With that in mind, Sengoku and other high-ranking officials put up a <a href="/wiki/Bounties" title="Bounties">bounty</a> of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>79,000,000 on her in order to help catch her.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Pursuit_of_the_Donquixote_Pirates">Pursuit of the Donquixote Pirates</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After Rosinante enlisted into the Marines and rose to the rank of commander, Sengoku assigned him with a mission to spy on the <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Pirates" title="Donquixote Pirates">Donquixote Pirates</a>, led by Rosinante's elder brother <a href="/wiki/Donquixote_Doflamingo" title="Donquixote Doflamingo">Donquixote Doflamingo</a>, and to make sure that children do not get involved with the pirate crew. Fourteen years before the current storyline, Rosinante contacted Sengoku and asked for permission to put his mission on hold, which Sengoku granted. He then accepted a request from <a href="/wiki/Vergo" title="Vergo">Vergo</a> to transfer to the <a href="/wiki/G-5" title="G-5">G-5</a> base, noting the progress he had made in the one year since he had joined the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Six months after Rosinante left the Donquixote Pirates, Sengoku contacted him again and was surprised that he was informed of the <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">Ope Ope no Mi</a> from his brother. Sengoku then informed Rosinante of a trade that was going to occur on <a href="/wiki/Rubeck_Island" title="Rubeck Island">Rubeck Island</a> in three weeks and Rosinante informed the admiral of Doflamingo's plans to steal the <a href="/wiki/Ope_Ope_no_Mi" title="Ope Ope no Mi">Ope Ope no Mi</a> and that the crew would be on <a href="/wiki/Swallow_Island" title="Swallow Island">Swallow Island</a> three days before the exchange. Sengoku then made plans to ambush the Donquixote Pirates on Swallow Island and warned Rosinante not to go anywhere near there.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After discovering Rosinante's death, Sengoku grieved.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At some point afterwards Sengoku meet <a href="/wiki/X_Drake" title="X Drake">X Drake</a>, who fled from his father's crew during the incident, and took him in, eventually seeing him as a son, just like Rosinante previously. <sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometimes afterwards, Sengoku rose to the rank of <a href="/wiki/Marine_Ranks#Fleet_Admiral" title="Marine Ranks">Fleet Admiral</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Sky_Island_Saga">Sky Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jaya_Arc">Jaya Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D42&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> had been defeated by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> and stripped of his rank as a <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a>, Sengoku was called in to discuss Crocodile's replacement in <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, along with the various Marine officers attending there and whoever among the Seven Warlords of the Sea decided to show up. He showed up late and caught Doflamingo <a href="/wiki/Ito_Ito_no_Mi" title="Ito Ito no Mi">messing around</a> with some of the Marine officials attending the meeting. Seeing the pirate's actions, he told him to stop immediately. With that settled, he apologized for being late, greeted everyone, and started the meeting.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png/revision/latest?cb=20230806151340" class="image"><img alt="Seven Warlords of the Sea Meeting at Mary Geoise" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Seven Warlords of the Sea Meeting at Mary Geoise.png" data-image-key="Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230806151340" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png/revision/latest?cb=20230806151340" class="image"><img alt="Seven Warlords of the Sea Meeting at Mary Geoise" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230806151340" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="158" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Seven Warlords of the Sea Meeting at Mary Geoise.png" data-image-key="Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/20/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230806151340" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea_Meeting_at_Mary_Geoise.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The meeting in Mary Geoise.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While Sengoku discussed some further formalities with Doflamingo, he and the others were shocked by <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>'s sudden appearance in the meeting. Sengoku and everyone else were then later interrupted by the appearance of <a href="/wiki/Laffitte" title="Laffitte">Laffitte</a>, who had somehow snuck into the meeting room. As Sengoku was told of the identity of this newcomer, Laffitte suggested a perfect candidate to replace Crocodile, <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Marshall D. Teach</a>. Having never heard of Teach before, Sengoku told Laffitte that an unknown pirate without a reputation would not be much use as a Warlord of the Sea. Laffitte, however, told Sengoku that he and the rest of his crew already had a plan to make Teach famous. With that, Laffitte left Sengoku and the other people attending the meeting and told them to remember his crew's name, the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_7_Saga">Water 7 Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D43&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-Enies_Lobby_Arc">Post-Enies Lobby Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D44&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Following the destruction of <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a>, Sengoku learned some startling information about one of the prominent players involved. Garp accidentally informed Sengoku that Luffy was his grandson. This revelation annoyed Sengoku because not only did Garp withhold such information, but also because he did not capture Luffy while he was in <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>. Sengoku ordered Garp to return to Water 7 to capture Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Saga">Thriller Bark Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Thriller_Bark_Arc">Thriller Bark Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Following the news of Warlord of the Sea <a href="/wiki/Gecko_Moria" title="Gecko Moria">Gecko Moria</a>'s defeat, Sengoku was in Mary Geoise with Garp and <a href="/wiki/Bartholomew_Kuma" title="Bartholomew Kuma">Bartholomew Kuma</a>. He was very angry that Kuma did not eliminate the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> and return with Luffy's head as proof of completion, revealing himself as the one who placed the termination order for the pirate crew. He also voiced concern about their increasing proximity to <a href="/wiki/Marine_Headquarters" title="Marine Headquarters">Marine Headquarters</a> and commented on how Luffy tended to get into one troublesome incident after another. Garp also annoyed him when he talked about tea and crackers instead of showing concern over his grandson's progress.<sup id="cite_ref-c490_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c490-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> 
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Summit_War_Saga">Summit War Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Strong_World">One Piece Film: Strong World</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Sengoku_Strong_World.png/revision/latest?cb=20230522014546" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Strong World" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Strong World.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Strong_World.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Sengoku_Strong_World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230522014546" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Sengoku_Strong_World.png/revision/latest?cb=20230522014546" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Strong World" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Sengoku_Strong_World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230522014546" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Strong World.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Strong_World.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b3/Sengoku_Strong_World.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230522014546" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Strong_World.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku during Shiki's attack on Marineford.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a> returned from his 20-year disappearance, he attacked Marineford using his powers to levitate and hurl fleets of ships at the island as a warning to the Marines. Sengoku was surprised he was still alive after all this time. After Shiki's surprising defeat at the hands of Luffy days later, Sengoku lamented on how the Marines were useless and they had been saved by pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Sabaody_Archipelago_Arc">Sabaody Archipelago Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku was greatly irritated by Luffy's attack on <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Noble</a> Saint <a href="/wiki/Charlos" title="Charlos">Charlos</a> and for "taking hostage" <a href="/wiki/Rosward" title="Rosward">his father</a> and <a href="/wiki/Shalria" title="Shalria">sister</a>. Seeing this, Admiral <a href="/wiki/Borsalino" title="Borsalino">Kizaru</a> offered to go to <a href="/wiki/Sabaody_Archipelago" title="Sabaody Archipelago">Sabaody Archipelago</a> himself to handle the problem with Sengoku's permission.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Amazon_Lily_Arc">Amazon Lily Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>At Marine Headquarters, Sengoku received the report that Vice Admiral <a href="/wiki/Momonga" title="Momonga">Momonga</a> had managed to "convince" Pirate Empress <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a> to follow up on the mandatory summons of the government. Sengoku was pleased by this as he acknowledged Hancock's strength but was also troubled that <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> refused to cooperate with them and was prepared to lose his status, fighting the Marines instead of <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Whitebeard</a>.
</p><p>Afterwards, an official told him of the number of pirates that Admiral Kizaru managed to capture at Sabaody and at least five hundred pirates were to be sent to <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>. Sengoku was irritated for being bothered for such a reason and asked to be informed only of matters relating to Whitebeard. In the same manner, he brushed off the matter of the incident with Saint Charlos, saying it was a matter for the admirals. He then asked where Garp was and was annoyed upon learning that he left for Impel Down a while ago. He then received news that Whitebeard's main ship, the <a href="/wiki/Moby_Dick" title="Moby Dick">Moby Dick</a>, was on the move and that all twenty-three patrol ships were decimated. He ordered extreme caution even at Impel Down.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Impel_Down_Arc">Impel Down Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230507213433" class="image"><img alt="Garp and Sengoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Garp_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f9/Garp_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230507213433" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_and_Sengoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku blaming Garp for Luffy's actions in Impel Down.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>To Sengoku's great displeasure, he received information that Luffy had broken into Impel Down and, putting the dots together, Sengoku correctly deduced that Luffy's invasion within the great prison itself was to rescue <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a> from execution in the critical time when they were supposed to be preparing for war against Whitebeard. Garp, however, found it amusing that his grandson would go to such lengths simply to rescue Ace. Sengoku angrily told Garp that no one had attempted anything so atrocious in the history of Impel Down, since twenty-two years prior to current events, and was annoyed that the one who would do it was Garp's grandson.
</p><p>Sengoku also said to Garp that had he not been the "Hero of the Marines", he would have held Garp personally responsible for his family's actions. Garp simply replied that the life of an old man would not atone for Luffy's transgressions.<sup id="cite_ref-MonkeyGrudge_15-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-MonkeyGrudge-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Blackbeard stole a Marine ship with his crew and broke into Impel Down, Sengoku looked distraught at the news.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Marineford_Arc">Marineford Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330005410" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Reveals Ace&#39;s Father" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Reveals Ace&#39;s Father.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330005410" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330005410" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Reveals Ace&#39;s Father" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330005410" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Reveals Ace&#39;s Father.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/07/Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330005410" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Reveals_Ace%27s_Father.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku reveals who Ace's father is.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Three hours prior to Ace's execution, Sengoku told Garp that he would reveal Ace's origins to the world,<sup id="cite_ref-Ace_father_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ace_father-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> which Garp allowed. Sengoku then revealed to his subordinates that Ace's father was none other than Gol D. Roger, the Pirate King. He later witnessed the arrival of Whitebeard and <a href="/wiki/Whitebeard_Pirates" title="Whitebeard Pirates">his allies</a>. According to Whitebeard, they had not seen each other in decades. When Whitebeard began his attack, Sengoku stated that Whitebeard ate the <a href="/wiki/Gura_Gura_no_Mi" title="Gura Gura no Mi">Gura Gura no Mi</a> and that he had the power to destroy the world.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Following several attacks from both sides, he proclaimed that the war had begun.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Even though pirates had breached the outer defenses. Sengoku was unbothered by the news and continued with his plan to execute Ace before the scheduled 3:00&#160;p.m. When Garp sat on the execution platform and was torn between family and duty, Sengoku warned him not to do anything foolish or he would suffer the consequences.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Luffy's unceremonious self-introduction into the <a href="/wiki/Summit_War_of_Marineford" title="Summit War of Marineford">Summit War of Marineford</a> had Sengoku apoplectic, going so far as screaming at Garp for having his family intruding in the World Government's affairs again. Sengoku only got angrier when Jinbe loudly declared his resignation from the Warlord of the Sea title. When asked by Kizaru if executions were in order for each and every last one of the Impel Down escapees, Sengoku wholeheartedly agreed and gave the order to attack.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> When Luffy declared that he was Ace's brother, which brought the question of how Roger can have a second son after he died before Ace's birth and Rouge dying shortly after the birth, Sengoku revealed to the world that Luffy was not only Ace's adoptive brother but is also <a href="/wiki/Revolutionary_Army" title="Revolutionary Army">Revolutionary</a> <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Dragon" title="Monkey D. Dragon">Dragon</a>'s son, making Luffy another dangerous future element.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Whitebeard split his forces rather than focusing them all in the bay, Sengoku realized that Whitebeard had sensed the Fleet Admiral's ruse but believed that the Emperor's intuition would not be enough to save him.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Meanwhile, Sengoku had ordered Akainu to deceive <a href="/wiki/Squard" title="Squard">Squard</a>, one of Whitebeard's allies, telling him that Whitebeard had sold out every one of his allies to the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Once their preparations were complete, Sengoku gave the order to cut the video broadcasting as an army of <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifista</a>—lead by <a href="/wiki/Sentomaru" title="Sentomaru">Sentomaru</a>—appeared at the mouth of the bay.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Even though the pirates were not all in the bay as planned, Sengoku still ordered the Pacifistas to attack the rear and also ordered the withdrawal of Marines off of the ice and into the plaza. Once the broadcast was ended, the Marines planned to raise the siege wall and execute Ace. However, <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy</a> had stolen one of the <a href="/wiki/Den_Den_Mushi#Visual_Den_Den_Mushi" title="Den Den Mushi">Visual Den Den Mushi</a> to broadcast his own fame as a member of the <a href="/wiki/Roger_Pirates" title="Roger Pirates">Roger Pirates</a>, so Sengoku had to delay Ace's execution and ordered the Marines to shoot down Buggy and his crew.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As part of the plan to deceive Squard, the Pacifistas attacked all non-Marines in the bay except members of the Whitebeard Pirates, and because of his hatred towards Roger (and by extension, his son Ace), Squard believed Akainu's words and attacked Whitebeard, stabbing him in the chest. Everything went according to Sengoku's plans, except for the fact that the whole world had seen everything happening thanks to Buggy's Den Den Mushi. In order to prevent him from broadcasting any more of the battle, Sengoku ordered Aokiji to <a href="/wiki/Hie_Hie_no_Mi" title="Hie Hie no Mi">freeze</a> him, the Den Den Mushi, and the Impel Down prisoners with him.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Whitebeard himself entered the battle and quaked the whole island, Sengoku ordered the raising of the siege wall; however, <a href="/wiki/Little_Oars_Jr." title="Little Oars Jr.">Little Oars Jr.</a>'s unconscious body held down a section. Sengoku then ordered Akainu to melt the ice underneath the pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Sengoku flinched when one of Whitebeard's shockwaves slammed against the wall but was unable to break it. His order to commence Ace's execution spurred Luffy into hurtling himself over the siege wall and landing in front of the execution platform, at which Sengoku grimaced.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> Sengoku then ordered for Ace's execution, but the executioners were attacked by Crocodile, much to Sengoku's surprise.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330005426" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Prepares For Battle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="325" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Prepares For Battle.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330005426" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330005426" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Prepares For Battle" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330005426" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="325" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Prepares For Battle.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c4/Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330005426" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Prepares_For_Battle.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku prepares to fight.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Oars Jr. had helped breach the siege wall with the newly revealed ship, which allowed the Whitebeard Pirates access into the main plaza, Sengoku stated that he would not be able to sit and watch anymore. He rolled up his sleeves and assumed that he would soon go into battle himself.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Marco" title="Marco">Marco</a> <a href="/wiki/Tori_Tori_no_Mi,_Model:_Phoenix" title="Tori Tori no Mi, Model: Phoenix">flew</a> at the execution platform, Garp, without an order from Sengoku, moved from his spot and punched the Whitebeard Commander.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sengoku watched as Ace was moved to tears by the sacrifice everyone was willing to make for him.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> After Marco and <a href="/wiki/Jozu" title="Jozu">Jozu</a> were grievously injured, Sengoku ordered the Marines to focus on Whitebeard, but the Emperor refused to die until he could secure a future for his "children". Telling Whitebeard to see their future as it was, Sengoku ordered for another pair of executioners to proceed with executing Ace. Luffy then unleashed a wave of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, which knocked out the executioners. Sengoku was shocked at this sudden burst of Haki.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20231026215527" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Attacks Luffy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Attacks Luffy.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231026215527" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png/revision/latest?cb=20231026215527" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Attacks Luffy" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231026215527" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Attacks Luffy.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/57/Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20231026215527" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Attacks_Luffy.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku strikes an inflated Luffy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Luffy, thanks to <a href="/wiki/Inazuma" title="Inazuma">Inazuma</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Choki_Choki_no_Mi" title="Choki Choki no Mi">powers</a>, managed to reach the execution platform,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> Sengoku complained about Garp hesitating and letting his grandson pass through him, declaring that even he was a father. Then, when Luffy tried to free his brother, Sengoku angrily transformed into <a href="/wiki/Hito_Hito_no_Mi,_Model:_Daibutsu" title="Hito Hito no Mi, Model: Daibutsu">his giant form</a>, declaring he would carry out the execution himself. As Sengoku attacked Luffy, the latter activated <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_3_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 3 Techniques">Gear 3</a>, which surprised Sengoku, seeing that Luffy's body size increased. Sengoku's attack was stopped by Luffy's Gigant Fusen, supplemented by <a href="/wiki/Galdino" title="Galdino">Mr. 3</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Doru_Doru_no_Mi#Techniques" title="Doru Doru no Mi">Candle Wall defense</a>. The execution platform was destroyed by Sengoku's massive punch and the fleet admiral fell to the ground with the pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Ace had been freed, Sengoku was ashamed of himself for allowing Ace to escape in his presence. As Whitebeard was reducing Marineford to ruins,<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> Sengoku told his men that Whitebeard was the threat for the moment.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010028" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Holds Down Garp" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Holds Down Garp.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010028" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010028" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Holds Down Garp" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010028" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Holds Down Garp.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b1/Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010028" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Holds_Down_Garp.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku pins Garp down.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After Akainu had killed Ace, an enraged Garp expressed a desire to kill the admiral in revenge. To prevent him from acting on this desire, Sengoku pinned Garp down to the ground, calling him a fool.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> When Akainu blasted off a portion of Whitebeard's head, Whitebeard still continued to shatter the Marine Headquarters, and Sengoku was shocked that the great pirate could still have so much power.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sengoku's shock became mixed with fury when the <a href="/wiki/Blackbeard_Pirates" title="Blackbeard Pirates">Blackbeard Pirates</a> arrived on the battlefield, with many legendary prisoners from Impel Down standing on the execution scaffold. Sengoku's fury only intensified when he learned that Blackbeard only wanted the Warlord of the Sea title to break into Impel Down to recruit those prisoners and that he had discarded the title.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When Whitebeard was saying his last words about the <a href="/wiki/Will_of_D." title="Will of D.">Will of D.</a>, Sengoku showed great fear and was furious with Whitebeard because he revealed to the entire world that <a href="/wiki/One_Piece" title="One Piece">One Piece</a> truly existed. After Whitebeard had taken his final breath, Sengoku witnessed Blackbeard and Whitebeard disappearing under a black cloth, and later Blackbeard coming out of it after somehow stealing the powers of the Gura Gura no Mi from his former captain and using them to attack the already crumbling Marineford.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20220825030710" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Attacks the Blackbeard Pirates" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Attacks the Blackbeard Pirates.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220825030710" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20220825030710" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Attacks the Blackbeard Pirates" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220825030710" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Attacks the Blackbeard Pirates.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/54/Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20220825030710" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Attacks_the_Blackbeard_Pirates.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku attacking the Blackbeard Pirates.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Blackbeard declared that this age was his and intended to start it off by sinking Marineford, Sengoku transformed into his Buddha form and delivered a powerful shockwave to the Blackbeard Pirates, sending the whole crew flying. He then warned Blackbeard not to go around spouting nonsense such as sinking the mighty fortress which represents <a href="/wiki/Justice" title="Justice">justice</a> and prepared to fight to defend the pride of the Marines.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Blackbeard taunted Sengoku and Garp, stating he would end their age just like he ended Whitebeard's.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The battle came to a halt by <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a>'s screaming for everyone to stop. Sengoku had listened to the young Marine's speech before he witnessed the arrival of <a href="/wiki/Shanks" title="Shanks">Shanks</a>, who stopped Akainu from killing Koby and stated to be in Marineford to end the war. After a short conversation with Shanks, Sengoku allowed him to take the bodies of Ace and Whitebeard, saying that he would take full responsibility for letting all the pirates on the battlefield go. He then told the Marines to tend to the wounded and that the war was over.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Post-War_Arc">Post-War Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010152" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Resting After the Battle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Resting After the Battle.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010152" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010152" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Resting After the Battle" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010152" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="134" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Resting After the Battle.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a6/Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010152" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Resting_After_the_Battle.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku resting after the battle.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sitting on a pile of rubble during the war's aftermath and covered in bandages from the injuries he had sustained at some point during the war, Sengoku was informed by <a href="/wiki/Brannew" title="Brannew">Brannew</a> about <a href="/wiki/Magellan" title="Magellan">Magellan</a>'s critical condition. Sengoku forbade Magellan from leaving his medical care to take responsibility for the mass breakouts or to commit suicide for his failure. He was also told about the situation in Impel Down Level 6, in which there were Level 6 prisoners missing from the prison other than the four Blackbeard took, despite Blackbeard ordering them to massacre each other and that he would take the winners as his new recruits.
</p><p>This led Sengoku to suspect that other Level 6 prisoners had also escaped. Sengoku told Brannew to distribute wanted posters immediately, as even one Level 6 prisoner getting into a nation could cause major casualties to its citizens. However, Brannew informed the fleet admiral that the World Government was trying to keep this breakout quiet in order to save face and to keep the faith of the people. This level of suppression greatly infuriated Sengoku.<sup id="cite_ref-c581_67-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c581-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010554" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Resigns from the Marines" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku Resigns from the Marines.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010554" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010554" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku Resigns from the Marines" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010554" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku Resigns from the Marines.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010554" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_Resigns_from_the_Marines.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku meets Kong and resigns.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Two weeks after the war, Sengoku approached Commander-in-Chief <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>, requesting resignation from his position as fleet admiral. Kong, though somewhat disappointed at this, accepted Sengoku's decision but assured him that both his and Garp's (who resigned earlier) records would remain untouched as an influential way of recruiting new Marines. Before departing, Sengoku suggested that Aokiji replace him as the next Marine fleet admiral.<sup id="cite_ref-c594_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c594-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Saga">Dressrosa Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><p><small>
<span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span></small></p><small><div style="float:right;">[<a href="#filmz">skip section</a>]</div></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece_Film:_Z">One Piece Film: Z</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D55&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku was shown at Marine Headquarters with Garp reflecting on the destruction of <a href="/wiki/Secon_Island" title="Secon Island">Secon Island</a> at the hands of the former Admiral <a href="/wiki/Z" title="Z">Z</a>. He remarked on how his past was very tragic and how destroying the island and putting innocent civilians in danger was unacceptable. Garp remarked that not everyone could see things separately like him. As Garp explained to <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a> and <a href="/wiki/Helmeppo" title="Helmeppo">Helmeppo</a> about Z's past, Sengoku stood silently reflecting on his former friend.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;" id="filmz"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Dressrosa_Arc">Dressrosa Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After Doflamingo's defeat, Sengoku discussed the news with <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> while snacking on some okaki.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Three days later, Sengoku and Tsuru arrived at <a href="/wiki/Dressrosa" title="Dressrosa">Dressrosa</a>. Sengoku cheerfully commented about Admiral <a href="/wiki/Issho" title="Issho">Fujitora</a>'s argument with Fleet Admiral Sakazuki and expressed how happy he was to not be Fleet Admiral anymore. They then met up with Admiral Fujitora and Sengoku laughed playfully at how Fujitora used a dice to determine his decision to not capture Luffy and Law. Sengoku was then greeted by the princess of the <a href="/wiki/Tontatta_Tribe" title="Tontatta Tribe">Tontatta Tribe</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mansherry" title="Mansherry">Mansherry</a>. After learning of <a href="/wiki/Chiyu_Chiyu_no_Mi" title="Chiyu Chiyu no Mi">her healing ability</a>, Sengoku offered to assist in healing the injured.<sup id="cite_ref-c796_20-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c796-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Law_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010809" class="image"><img alt="Law and Sengoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Law and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Law_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Law_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010809" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Law_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230330010809" class="image"><img alt="Law and Sengoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Law_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010809" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Law and Sengoku.png" data-image-key="Law_and_Sengoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Law_and_Sengoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230330010809" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Law_and_Sengoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Law and Sengoku reminiscing on Rosinante.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the Marines had been mobilized to pursue Luffy and <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Grand_Fleet" title="Straw Hat Grand Fleet">his allies</a>, Sengoku had a private conversation with Law concerning Rosinante near the eastern port. After discussing how much Rosinante meant to each of them, Law revealed himself to be a "<a href="/wiki/Will_of_D." title="Will of D.">D.</a>" and asked Sengoku about it. Sengoku was surprised at the revelation but did not answer the question. Sengoku then told Law to live his life as Rosinante wanted. Their conversation ended when Issho used his gravity ability to lift all the rubble in Dressrosa in preparation to strike Luffy's allies at the eastern port.<sup id="cite_ref-c798_12-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c798-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After Fujitora had allowed Luffy and his allies to escape, Sengoku appeared behind him, saying that he heard him thanking Luffy.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> After leaving Dressrosa, Sengoku and the Marines escorted Doflamingo. Sengoku asked Issho to apologize to Sakazuki, but he refused, saying that he still has his pride. Sometime later, a subordinate of <a href="/wiki/Kaidou" title="Kaidou">Kaidou</a>, <a href="/wiki/Jack" title="Jack">Jack</a>, attacked the Marine convoy in an attempt to retrieve Doflamingo.<sup id="cite_ref-c801_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c801-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Though he sank two of the Marine ships, Jack was ultimately defeated.<sup id="cite_ref-c806_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c806-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Whole_Cake_Island_Saga">Whole Cake Island Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D57&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Levely_Arc">Levely Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D58&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sengoku later returned to New Marineford. When <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a> was furious about Issho's presence at <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>, Sengoku jokingly commented that Sakazuki's job as fleet admiral must be difficult, much to Sakazuki's annoyance.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Saga">Wano Country Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D59&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece:_Stampede">One Piece: Stampede</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D60&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 200px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20210726121057" class="image"><img alt="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet.png" data-image-key="Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210726121057" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest?cb=20210726121057" class="image"><img alt="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210726121057" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="200" height="113" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Garp And Sengoku Talks About Douglas Bullet.png" data-image-key="Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/29/Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20210726121057" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Garp_And_Sengoku_Talks_About_Douglas_Bullet.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Sengoku and Garp talk about Douglas Bullet.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sengoku appears outside the Marine Headquarters, where Garp meets him, and begins to tell him about <a href="/wiki/Douglas_Bullet" title="Douglas Bullet">Douglas Bullet</a>'s past.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup>
<br style="clear:both;" />
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Wano_Country_Arc">Wano Country Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D61&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the abolishment of the Seven Warlords of the Sea system and the Marines learning of Big Mom and Kaidou's newly formed alliance, Sengoku participated in a meeting with many Marine officers. Sengoku told them about the <a href="/wiki/Rocks_Pirates" title="Rocks Pirates">Rocks Pirates</a>, along with their captain, <a href="/wiki/Rocks_D._Xebec" title="Rocks D. Xebec">Rocks D. Xebec</a>, who he remembered well. He then went into detail explaining the <a href="/wiki/God_Valley_Incident" title="God Valley Incident">God Valley Incident</a>, along with the history Garp had with <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Roger</a> facing the Rocks Pirates. Fleet Admiral Sakazuki then entered the room and said that the Marines were leaving Wano Country alone due to not having enough manpower to deal with both Big Mom and Kaidou. Sengoku and Sakazuki then discussed about Kouzuki Oden and the relationships he had with the Four Emperors.<sup id="cite_ref-c957_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c957-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Final_Saga">Final Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D62&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Egghead_Arc">Egghead Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D63&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sometime later, Sengoku and <a href="/wiki/Tsuru" title="Tsuru">Tsuru</a> were present at New Marineford, reading up on the news about <a href="/wiki/T_Bone" title="T Bone">T Bone</a> having been murdered by an unknown assassin motivated by the money rewarded by the <a href="/wiki/Cross_Guild" title="Cross Guild">Cross Guild</a>. Both were concerned with the threat the Marines were now facing from both pirates and common people. During their discussion, <a href="/wiki/Hina" title="Hina">Hina</a> joined them and informed them that <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D.
