Garp">Garp</a> was heading to <a href="/wiki/Hachinosu" title="Hachinosu">Hachinosu</a> to rescue <a href="/wiki/Koby" title="Koby">Koby</a>, to the duo's shock.<sup id="cite_ref-c1082_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1082-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> Later during the <a href="/wiki/Egghead_Incident" title="Egghead Incident">Egghead Incident</a>, Sengoku and Tsuru listened to <a href="/wiki/Vegapunk" title="Vegapunk">Vegapunk</a>'s broadcast while onboard her battleship.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Major_Battles">Major Battles</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D64&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<li>Sengoku vs. <a href="/wiki/Edward_Newgate" title="Edward Newgate">Edward Newgate</a> (unseen, several times)</li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D65&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_DX_Marine.png/revision/latest?cb=20130525045014" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku DX Marine" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="226" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Sengoku DX Marine.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_DX_Marine.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_DX_Marine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20130525045014" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_DX_Marine.png/revision/latest?cb=20130525045014" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku DX Marine" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_DX_Marine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20130525045014" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="226" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Sengoku DX Marine.png" data-image-key="Sengoku_DX_Marine.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/38/Sengoku_DX_Marine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20130525045014" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Sengoku_DX_Marine.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">One Piece DX Marine Sengoku.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Sengoku thus far has been featured in the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_DX_Figure" title="One Piece DX Figure">One Piece DX Figure</a> The Marines set, along in the One Piece Collection -Promise of the Marineford, and the One Piece Den Den Mushi Measuring Tape collection.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FSengoku%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D70&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 157px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Sengoku%27s_Goat.png/revision/latest?cb=20130629010151" class="image"><img alt="Sengoku&#39;s Goat" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="134" data-image-name="Sengoku&#39;s Goat.png" data-image-key="Sengoku%27s_Goat.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/46/Sengoku%27s_Goat.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20130629010151" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Sengoku's pet goat.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 157px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Bartolomeo%27s_Imagination_of_Sengoku_and_Tsuru.png/revision/latest?cb=20161221125616" class="image"><img alt="Bartolomeo&#39;s Imagination of Sengoku and Tsuru" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="92" data-image-name="Bartolomeo&#39;s Imagination of Sengoku and Tsuru.png" data-image-key="Bartolomeo%27s_Imagination_of_Sengoku_and_Tsuru.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Bartolomeo%27s_Imagination_of_Sengoku_and_Tsuru.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20161221125616" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Sengoku (on the left) and Tsuru in Bartolomeo's imagination.
</div></span></div>
<ul><li>Sengoku has a <a href="/wiki/Pet" title="Pet">pet</a> goat. The goat is often with Sengoku, including in a Marine base when Saul was ordered to attack Ohara,<sup id="cite_ref-c396_29-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c396-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> at the reunion after <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a>'s defeat,<sup id="cite_ref-debut_1-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> at the meeting in Mary Geoise after the events in <a href="/wiki/Thriller_Bark" title="Thriller Bark">Thriller Bark</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-c490_35-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c490-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> on the execution platform when Ace's parentage is revealed,<sup id="cite_ref-Ace_father_16-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Ace_father-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> and during the aftermath of the war.<sup id="cite_ref-c581_67-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c581-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> After the timeskip, the goat is on the Marine ship leaving Dressrosa.<sup id="cite_ref-c801_71-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c801-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> The goat was also present while Sengoku spoke to many Marines officers about the past of the Rocks Pirates.<sup id="cite_ref-c957_74-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c957-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup>The goat is seen again eating in the Marines' Cantina while Sengoku and Tsuru discuss Cross Guild.<sup id="cite_ref-c1082_75-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c1082-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Party" title="One Piece Party">One Piece Party</a>, <a href="/wiki/Sakazuki" title="Sakazuki">Sakazuki</a> jokingly said that the goat had the <b>Yagi Yagi no Mi</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ヤギヤギの実</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>, literally meaning "Goat Goat Fruit")</span><sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup></li></ul></li>
<li>When Sengoku and Tsuru were mentioned by <a href="/wiki/Bartolomeo" title="Bartolomeo">Bartolomeo</a>, they were shown in the latter's imagination, hardly resembling their real appearance at all.</li>
<li>"Sengoku" can be written in kanji as 戦国, meaning "warring states", a term borrowed from ancient Chinese to represent a period of history in Japan known as the "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sengoku_period" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sengoku period">Sengoku Period</a>", which was recorded to have had near constant military conflict with extensive use of naval forces.</li>
<li>Coincidentally, Sengoku shares his birthday, May 9, with <a href="/wiki/Kong" title="Kong">Kong</a>, his <a href="/wiki/Fleet_Admiral" class="mw-redirect" title="Fleet Admiral">Fleet Admiral</a> predecessor.</li>
<li>Sengoku is the first known <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a> user who has never been a pirate. He and <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Garp" title="Monkey D. Garp">Garp</a> are also the only known Marines to possess this type of Haki as well as the only known Marines capable of using all three forms of Haki.
<ul><li>He, <a href="/wiki/Eustass_Kid" title="Eustass Kid">Eustass Kid</a> and <a href="/wiki/Boa_Hancock" title="Boa Hancock">Boa Hancock</a> are the only characters confirmed to have Supreme King Haki, but never shown any usage of it yet in the manga. Kid had showcased it in the anime as well as in, with Hancock in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_4" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 4">Pirate Warriors 4</a></i>, thus making Sengoku the only Supreme King Haki user to so far not use it in any forms of media.</li></ul></li>
<li>Sengoku's motto is "Reigning Justice".<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Sengoku is the first known Marine admiral to not have had a codename, the second being the non-canon <a href="/wiki/Z" title="Z">Z</a>.</li>
<li>Sengoku's favorite food is Marines' okaki.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_7-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>
